In short, the service is not bad after experience, the facilities are a bit old, but better than expected.

2. The location is good: the core location of the CBD, the hotel is connected to China World Mall and the subway, and the transportation is convenient. If you go to Universal, you can go directly to the subway.
3. Good food: Juices and snacks are basically available all day in the executive lounge. The nasi lemak, poached eggs and noodles on the breakfast menu are delicious, and the meals during happy hour are also more delicate and not foolish, unlike some hotels The executive lounge is a mere formality.
4. Good hygiene: the room is very clean, the service auntie is very good, greets each other kindly, and cleans the room in the morning and afternoon.
5. High cost performance: I bought the "Hi FUN City in the City" package for parents and children. The package includes food, entertainment, parent-child room layout and executive lounge trea**ent. Super tall, the baby is very happy. It is recommended to choose this package for families with children who do not want to go out of Beijing and consider city vacations.
